    function getAdCookie(name) {
        var regex = new RegExp('(?:^|; )' + name + '=([^;]*)');
        var value = regex.exec(document.cookie);
        if (value && value.length > 1) {
            value = decodeURIComponent(value[1]);
        } else {
            value = "";
        }
        return value;
    }

    function conditionalTitanAdPushExternalReferrer(adUniqueName, cookieExternalReferrer) {

            }

<script>
    /**
     * Moves editbar from above container div to first item in the target div.
     */
    (function(){
        var $containerDiv = $("div.top-recommended-column.RecommendedPromo");
        var fixTargetDiv = "";
        $(function() {
            var endTime = new Date().getTime() + 30000; // try for 10 seconds max
            var moveToolbar = function() {
                if(new Date().getTime() > endTime || (!$containerDiv.length)) return;
                var $toolbar = $containerDiv.prev();
                if($toolbar.hasClass("cq-editbar-placeholder")) {
                    if (fixTargetDiv == "") {
                        $toolbar.prependTo($containerDiv.children().first());
                    } else {
                        $toolbar.prependTo($containerDiv.find(fixTargetDiv).first());
                    }
                } else {
                    window.setTimeout(moveToolbar, 250);
                }
            }
            moveToolbar();
        });
    })()
</script></section>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var membershipStatus = (function() {
        var userType = "unknown";

        if (typeof FFXHagrid !== "undefined" && FFXHagrid.isLoggedIn()) {
            try {
                FFXHagrid.getUserPlansProvider().getUserPlans(false, function(plans) {
                    if (typeof plans !== "undefined" && plans.length > 0) {
                        userType = "subscriber " + plans.join(",").toLowerCase();
                    } else {
                        userType = "member";
                    }
                });
            } catch (e) {
                userType ="member";
            }
        } else {
            userType = "visitor";
        }

        return userType;
    })();

    var memberID = (function() {
        var cookies = (document.cookie && document.cookie.length > 0) ? document.cookie.split(";") : [];
        for(var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
            var cookie = cookies[i].trim();
            var cookieName = cookie.split("=")[0];
            var cookieValue = cookie.split("=")[1];
            if (cookieName.indexOf("ffx_unique_id") === 0) {
                return cookieValue;
            }
        }
        return "unknown";
    })();

    if (s){
        // Brand:Site Section:Sub Section:Sub Section 2:Page Title:Asset ID
        s.pageName = "smh:Home:::Sydney Morning Herald homepage:"
        // Member ID (prop51)
        s.prop51 = memberID

        
            s.prop1 = "smh"
        
            s.prop2 = ""
        
            s.prop6 = ""
        
            s.prop7 = "Index"
        
            s.prop8 = " Index"
        
            s.prop31 = ""
        
            s.prop32 = "2015-04-12"
        

        if (window["FD"]) {
            if (typeof FD.s_prop24 !== "undefined") {
                s.prop24 = FD.s_prop24
            }
        }

        // OLG tracking
        if (typeof olgTracking !== "undefined") {
            if (s.events) {
                s.events += ",event21";
            } else {
                s.events = "event21";
            }
            s.eVar22 = s.prop1 + "-" + s.prop2 + "-" + olgTracking.provider + "-" + olgTracking.productType + "-" + olgTracking.location;
        }
        s.eVar57 = membershipStatus;

        // REF-5669, All the beacon firing will be controlled in DTM.
        // s.t();

        if (typeof window.analyticsFFX_TriggerLegecyBeacon != "undefined"
                && typeof window.analyticsFFX_TriggerLegecyBeacon === "function" ){
            window.analyticsFFX_TriggerLegecyBeacon(s);
        }
    }
</script>
